Withdrawal fees are subject to change depending on network conditions. If fees change rapidly after you make a withdrawal request, we may contact you about your withdrawal options.
Withdrawal fees include blockchain transfer fees and are outside our control. The minimum withdrawal amount is typically 2x the transaction fee.
For supported low-fee networks such as the Bitcoin Lightning Network, transaction fees and minimum withdrawal amounts are usually much lower than on-chain networks.
Please ensure that the wallet or exchange you are using supports %networkNames% transactions and that you are withdrawing on the correct network. You may permanently lose your assets if you send funds to an incompatible address or to a wallet that you do not control.

In our Bitcoin mining system, the key detail of each mining contract is its hashrate (mining speed), shown in the lower-right corner (for example, 2 GH/s).
In general, a higher hashrate can increase mining speed and may lead to faster reward progress. However, mining outcomes depend on real Bitcoin network conditions (including network hashrate/difficulty and other factors), so rewards are variable and not guaranteed.
Paid contracts may include a Continuity Multiplier, which can boost rewards credited from that contract while it remains active. The longer the contract stays active, the higher the continuity multiplier can grow under the current boost rules (subject to change). For example, a 2
 continuity multiplier would apply a 2
 boost to that contract's current base rewards under the current rules. This is an illustration only and not a promise of any specific amount or boost.
Because rewards depend on real network conditions and other factors, daily outcomes can be slightly higher or lower from day to day.

En konto med denne e-postadressen eksisterer allerede:
In our mining plans, the key factor is mining speed (hashrate), shown as values like 2 GH/s.
In general, a higher hashrate can increase mining speed and may lead to faster reward progress, but outcomes vary with Bitcoin network conditions and aren't guaranteed.
Paid plans may include a Continuity Boost that can grow over time while the plan stays active. Your account may also have a Loyalty Boost that grows as you obtain and use plans and applies across your active plans.
Continuity and loyalty boosts can stack together (for example, 2
 continuity and 2
 loyalty combine to a 4
 boost under the current rules). Boosts are app features that affect how rewards are credited in the app; rewards are variable and not guaranteed.

A more efficient solution is to split your build function into several widgets. This introduces a new context from which you can obtain the Scaffold. In this solution, you would have an outer widget that creates the Scaffold populated by instances of your new inner widgets, and then in these inner widgets you would use Scaffold.of().
A less elegant but more expedient solution is assign a GlobalKey to the Scaffold, then use the key.currentState property to obtain the ScaffoldState rather than using the Scaffold.of() function.

whiteMountainView titleMedium
From time to time we may adjust the hashrate amounts available for free, rewarded, or paid plans to keep the system sustainable and aligned with real Bitcoin network conditions, advertising revenue, capacity, and other factors. When demand or costs increase, the in-app cost of hashrate may rise, so for the same price (or via free/rewarded plans) you may receive less hashrate than before.
If the hashrate offered for watching ads seems lower after many ads in a row, this may be due to how ad partners, pacing, and our anti-abuse/operational limits allocate rewards. Taking a break and trying again later may result in a different offer.
When conditions are more favorable, we may be able to offer higher hashrate at the same or lower in-app cost.
Once you purchase or claim a free/rewarded plan, the hashrate shown for that plan remains same for its active duration, even if future offers change. However, reward outcomes remain variable and are not guaranteed.
